# <a name="com-error-codes-comadmin-filter-graphics"></a><span data-ttu-id="edaa9-104">Códigos de error COM (COMAdmin, filtro, gráficos)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="edaa9-104">COM Error Codes (COMADMIN, FILTER, GRAPHICS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="edaa9-105">En la tabla siguiente se proporciona una lista de códigos de error usados por las API basadas en COM.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="edaa9-105">The following table provides a list of error codes used by COM-based APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="edaa9-106">Si tiene problemas con la aplicación que está instalando o ejecutando, póngase en contacto con el servicio de soporte al cliente para ver el software que muestra el mensaje de error.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="edaa9-106">If you are experiencing difficulty with an application you are installing or running, contact customer support for the software that is displaying the error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="edaa9-107">Para obtener soporte técnico para un producto de Microsoft, vaya a [https://support.microsoft.com](https://www.microsoft.com/?ref=go) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="edaa9-107">To obtain support for a Microsoft product, go to [https://support.microsoft.com](https://www.microsoft.com/?ref=go).</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="edaa9-108">Constante o valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="edaa9-108">Constant/value</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | <span data-ttu-id="edaa9-109">Descripción</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="edaa9-109">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
|:--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|:--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span id="COMADMIN_E_OBJECTERRORS"></span><span id="comadmin_e_objecterrors"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="edaa9-110"><dt>**COMadmin \_ E \_ OBJECTERRORS**</dt> <dt>0x80110401</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="edaa9-110"><dt>**COMADMIN\_E\_OBJECTERRORS**</dt> <dt>0x80110401</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                                                                                                  | <span data-ttu-id="edaa9-111">Se produjeron errores al obtener acceso a uno o más objetos: la colección ErrorInfo puede tener más detalles</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="edaa9-111">Errors occurred accessing one or more objects - the ErrorInfo collection may have more detail</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
